< review>
We made an appointment in Watsonville since it was the only DMV office that was not booked a month or more out. The staff was very friendly and helpful. There were sufficient staff members on site to help with all sorts of questions and since we had an appointment, we were called in right away (after I asked how this worked at this DMV since there was no appointment line). The line was not long anyway. The office is small but very efficient. Maybe we got a good day, but it was one of the best, smoothest and most efficient DMV experiences ever. Well worth the trip to experience such a short wait and good service.</review>

{'time': 1522276204763, 'text': 'Hello Lisa,\nI know that you are not, and have never been a client of TVAH.\n\nAlthough there are facilities that will take your money and give the vaccine without taking note of the medical condition of the patient, we will not. That is not our protocol.
